***booby.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a> (70818)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>17th century. <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spanish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Spanish language">Spanish</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="es"><a href = vnd.unilang:bobo.html>bobo</a></i>, from <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">balbus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stammering</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">boobies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A stupid person.
<ul><li><b>1773</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oliver_Goldsmith" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Oliver Goldsmith"><a href = vnd.unilang:oliver.html>Oliver</a> Goldsmith</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/She_Stoops_to_Conquer" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:She Stoops to Conquer">She Stoops to Conquer</a></i>, Act I, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/files/383/383-h/383-h.htm">[1]</a>
<dl><dd>The daughter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> to be well-bred and beautiful; the son an awkward <b><a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a></b>, reared up and spoiled at his mother's apron-string.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1854</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_David_Thoreau" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry David Thoreau"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> David Thoreau</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walden" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Walden">Walden</a></i>, New York: Thomas Y. Crowell amp; Co., 1910, Chapter I, p. 74, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://archive.org/details/walden01thor">[2]</a>
<dl><dd>As for the Pyramids, there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> nothing to wonder at in them so much as the fact that so many <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> could be found degraded enough to spend their <a href = vnd.unilang:lives.html>lives</a> constructing a tomb for some ambitious <b><a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a></b>, whom it would have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> wiser and manlier to have drowned in the Nile, and then given his body to the dogs.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1942</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Emily_Carr" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Emily Carr">Emily Carr</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Book_of_Small" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Book of Small">The Book of Small</a></i>, "How Lizzie <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a> Shamed Right Through," <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.net.au/ebooks04/0400201.txt">[3]</a>
<dl><dd>She knotted our ribbons very tightly so that <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> should not lose them,—they pulled the little hairs under our curls and made us "ooch" and wriggle. Then <a href = vnd.unilang:dede.html>Dede</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> us little smacks and called us <b>boobies</b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>Any of various large tropical seabirds from the genera <i>Sula</i> and <i>Papasula</i> in the gannet family Sulidae, traditionally considered to be stupid.
<ul><li><b>1638</b> Herbert, <a href = vnd.unilang:sir.html>Sir</a> Thomas <i>Some years travels into divers parts of Asia and Afrique</i>
<dl><dd>At which time, ſome <b>Boobyes</b>, weary of flight, made our Ship their pearch, an animall ſo ſimple as ſuffers any to take her without feare, as if a ſtupid ſenſe made her careleſſe of danger...</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1839</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charles_Darwin" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charles Darwin">Charles Darwin</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Voyage_of_the_Beagle" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Voyage of the Beagle">The Voyage of the Beagle</a></i>, Chapter I, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gutenberg.org/cache/epub/944/pg944-images.html">[4]</a>
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>We</a> found on St. Paul's only two <a href = vnd.unilang:kinds.html>kinds</a> of birds—the <b><a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a></b> and the noddy. The former <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a species of gannet, and the latter a tern. Both are of a tame and stupid disposition, and are so unaccustomed to visitors, that I could have killed any number of them with my geological hammer.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>In the game of <a href = vnd.unilang:croquet.html>croquet</a>, a ball that <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> not passed through the first wicket.
<ul><li><b>1863</b>, Mayne Reid, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:croquet.html>Croquet</a></i>, London: C.J. <a href = vnd.unilang:skeet.html>Skeet</a>, p. 33, <a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://books.google.ca/books?id=zzUCAAAAQAAJamp;printsec=frontcoverv=onepageamp;qamp;f=false">[5]</a>
<dl><dd>A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a></b> may <i>displace</i> another <b><a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a></b> or a bridged ball by roquet, ricochet, or concussion.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">stupid person</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> Thesaurus:fool</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">large tropical seabird</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">sulid</span></li></ul>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">boobies</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">boobying</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">boobied</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To behave stupidly; to act like a <a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a>.
<ul><li><b>1824</b> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Washington_Irving" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Washington Irving">Washington Irving</a>, "Proclamation", <i>Salmagundi</i> volume 1:
<dl><dd>Who lounge and who loot, and who <b><a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a></b> about, / No knowledge within, and no manners without;</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To install a <a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a> on or at (something); to attack (someone) with a <a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trap.html>trap</a>.
<ul><li><b>1976</b> "Weekly Almanac", <i>Jet</i> volume 22, page 44:
<dl><dd>Self <b>Boobied</b>. Donald E. Campbell of Merritt Island, Fla., accidentally tripped on one of the shotgun shell <a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:traps.html>traps</a> he <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> installed</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the earlier form <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bubby</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:booby.html>booby</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">boobies</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A woman’s breast.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <i>see</i> Thesaurus:<span class="Latn" lang="en">breast</span></span></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1934</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Miller" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Miller"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> Miller</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tropic_of_Cancer_(novel)" class="extiw" title="w:Tropic of Cancer (novel)">Tropic of Cancer</a></i>:
<dl><dd>At ten <a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a>’clock she <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> lying on the <a href = vnd.unilang:divan.html>divan</a> with her <b>boobies</b> in her hands.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1968</b>,  “Ain'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> Got No, I Got Life”, in  <cite>'Nuff <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>Said</a>!</cite>, performed by <a href = vnd.unilang:nina.html>Nina</a> Simone:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Got my neck, got my <b>boobies</b> / Got my heart, got my soul / Got my back, I got my sex</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>2008</b>, Richard Uhlig, <i>Boy Minus Girl</i>:
<dl><dd>She <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> beyond hot: her long, black, <a href = vnd.unilang:curly.html>curly</a> hair <a href = vnd.unilang:cascades.html>cascades</a> around her naked <b>boobies</b>!</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

***boog.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boog.html>boog</a> (5325)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bōge</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bogo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*bugô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boog.html>boog</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bogen.html>bogen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boogje.html>boogje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A bow (ranged weapon).</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">geometry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An arc.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An arch.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">architecture</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The arch of a foot.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">voetboog</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***boogbal.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boogbal.html>boogbal</a> (65791)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boog.html>boog</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">arch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ball</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boogbal.html>boogbal</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boogbal.html>boogballen</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ball sports<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncommon</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:lob.html>lob</a></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">arching shot or pass</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***booger.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:booger.html>booger</a> (54927)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Alteration of the English dialectal <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> <i>buggard</i> (<i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bug</i> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-ard</i>), <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">boggart</i> or <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">boggard</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:booger.html>booger</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boogers.html>boogers</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A piece of solid or semisolid mucus in or removed from a nostril.
<ul><li><b>2006</b>, Strapping Young Lad, "Far Beyond Metal", <i>The New Black</i>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Now in the <a href = vnd.unilang:halls.html>halls</a> of the necro lord / Flash of fear when he <a href = vnd.unilang:sees.html>sees</a> my sword / Raped his woman, smoked his bone / Leave a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:booger.html>booger</a></b> underneath his throne!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Something suggestive of this material.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2017</b> July 7,  Ignatiy Vishnevetsky,  “The ambitious War For The Planet Of The <a href = vnd.unilang:apes.html>Apes</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ends.html>ends</a> up surrendering to formula”, in  <cite>The Onion AV Club</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.avclub.com/review/ambitious-war-planet-apes-ends-surrendering-formul-257757">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">The latter <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> discovered by <a href = vnd.unilang:caesar.html>Caesar</a>, Maurice, and their <a href = vnd.unilang:compadres.html>compadres</a> living in a crumbling, snow-packed ski lodge, its antler chandeliers hung with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boogers.html>boogers</a></b> of ice in a mockery of humanity’s pretensions of alpha-predator-hood.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/United_States" class="extiw" title="w:United States">US</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A thing; especially a problematic or difficult thing.</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boogschutter.html>boogschutter</a> (25016)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boog.html>boog</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:schutter.html>schutter</a></i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bôom</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bōm</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*baumaz</i>.

***boomer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> boomer (7816)</h1><br></body> 
***boomerang.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a> (94976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dharug_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dharug language">Dharug</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="xdk">bumariny</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">boomerangs</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:flat.html>flat</a> curved airfoil, that spins about an axis perpendicular to the direction of flight, that <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> originally used in various parts of the world as hunting <a href = vnd.unilang:weapons.html>weapons</a> or, in returnable <a href = vnd.unilang:types.html>types</a>, for sports or training.
<ul><li><b>1884</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Andrew_Lang" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Andrew Lang">Andrew <a href = vnd.unilang:lang.html>Lang</a></a>, <i>Star Myths</i> in <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Custom_and_Myth/Star_Myths" class="extiw" title="s:Custom and Myth/Star Myths">Custom and Myth</a></i>,
<dl><dd>Some resemblance to terrestrial <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a>, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> true, everyone can behold in the heavens. <i>Corona</i>, for example, <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> like a crown, or, as the Australian black fellows know, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> like a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a></b>, and <a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> can understand why they give it the name of that curious curved missile.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1897</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:warren.html>Warren</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bert.html>Bert</a> Kimberly,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/History_of_West_Australia" class="extiw" title="s:History of West Australia">History of West Australia</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">With <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a></b> and spear they hunted the kangaroo and emu, and fought their battles beneath the <a href = vnd.unilang:eucalyptus.html>eucalyptus</a> forests; their <a href = vnd.unilang:minds.html>minds</a>, fresh, untroubled, contented, oblivious alike of noble ideals and philosophic principles.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><b>1961</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Charlie_Drake" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Charlie Drake"><a href = vnd.unilang:charlie.html>Charlie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:drake.html>Drake</a></a>, song, <i>My <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>Boomerang</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:won.html>Won</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> Come Back</i>,
<dl><dd>"Don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> worry, boy, I know the trick, / And to you I'm <a href = vnd.unilang:gonna.html>gonna</a> show it. / If you want your <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a></b> to come back, / Well first you've got to... throw it."</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>A breakdancing move in which the performer walks on his or her hands while <a href = vnd.unilang:keeping.html>keeping</a> the <a href = vnd.unilang:legs.html>legs</a> raised off the ground.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:kylie.html>kylie</a></span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="list-switcher" data-toggle-category="derived terms"><div class="derivedterms term-list ul-column-count" data-column-count="3" style="background-color: F8F8FF;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:baby.html>baby</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a> child</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a> effect</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">boomeranger</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a> kid</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a> pillow</span></li></ul></div><div class="list-switcher-element" data-showtext=" show more ▼ " data-hidetext=" show less  " style="display: none;"> </div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">boomerangs</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">boomeranging</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">boomeranged</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To return or rebound unexpectedly, especially when the result <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> undesired; to backfire.
<ul><li><b>1882</b> March 7, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arthur_Conan_Doyle" class="extiw" title="w:Arthur Conan Doyle">Arthur Conan Doyle</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Stark_Munro_Letters/Letter_6" class="extiw" title="s:The Stark Munro Letters/Letter 6">The <a href = vnd.unilang:stark.html>Stark</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:munro.html>Munro</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:letters.html>Letters</a></a></i>,
<dl><dd>"Well, there must be some flaw about this," I suggested. "If your magnet <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> so strong as all that, you would have your own broadside <b>boomeranging</b> back upon you."</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1899</b> November, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/%22Showin%27_Off%22" class="extiw" title="s:quot;Showin |  Offquot;">"Showin' Off"</a></i> in <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Harper%27s_Magazine" class="extiw" title="w:Harper | s Magazine">Harper's New Monthly Magazine</a></i>, Volume 99, Number 594,
<dl><dd>"<a href = vnd.unilang:oh.html>Oh</a>," they yelled, "you could, <a href = vnd.unilang:eh.html>eh</a>? Well, let's see you do it, then! Let's see you do it! Let's see you do it! Now!" In a <a href = vnd.unilang:moment.html>moment</a> the crew of little spectators <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> gibing at Horace. The blow that would make Jimmie's humiliation complete! Instead, it <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <b>boomeranged</b> Horace into the mud.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1985</b> February 2, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ronald_Reagan" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Ronald Reagan">Ronald Reagan</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/Presidential_Radio_Address_-_2_February_1985" class="extiw" title="s:Presidential Radio Address - 2 February 1985">Presidential Radio Address</a></i>,
<dl><dd>Our future economic success depends on the economy growing faster than government spending. That's why raising taxes would <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boomerang.html>boomerang</a></b>. Economic growth would slow, revenues would decline, and the budget deficit would swell.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To travel in a curved path.
<ul><li><b>1894</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Henry_Lawson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Henry Lawson"><a href = vnd.unilang:henry.html>Henry</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lawson.html>Lawson</a></a>, <i>The Mystery of <a href = vnd.unilang:dave.html>Dave</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:regan.html>Regan</a></i> in <i><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://gutenberg.net.au/ebooks06/0607911.txt">Short <a href = vnd.unilang:stories.html>Stories</a> in Prose and Verse</a></i>,
<dl><dd>He <a href = vnd.unilang:said.html>said</a> that to the horse as it <b>boomeranged</b> off again and <a href = vnd.unilang:broke.html>broke</a> away through the scrub.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

***boomgaard.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:boomgaard.html>boomgaard</a> (19910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boomgaert</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">bōmgardo</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boom.html>boom</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tree</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">gaard</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">garden</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomgaard.html>boomgaard</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomgaarden.html>boomgaarden</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boomgaardje.html>boomgaardje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">boosheit</i>. </p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boosheid.html>boosheid</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>anger
<dl><dd><i>In <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:boosheid.html>boosheid</a></b> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:scheurde.html>scheurde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> contract <a href = vnd.unilang:doormidden.html>doormidden</a>.</i></dd>
<dd><i>In his anger he tore up the contract.</i></dd></dl></li></ol>

***booswicht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:booswicht.html>booswicht</a> (76909)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boos.html>boos</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">evil</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">living being</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:booswicht.html>booswicht</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:booswichten.html>booswichten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:booswicht.html>booswichtje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>wicked person, felon</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>In Dutch, compound <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> normally always take the gender of the latter component of the compound. In this case, the latter component <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wicht.html>wicht</a></i>, a neuter word, which would render the compound neuter. However, due to the word being almost always used to refer to a male person, it <a href = vnd.unilang:takes.html>takes</a> the masculine gender.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:booswicht.html>booswicht</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:schurk.html>schurk</a></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synoniemen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:synoniemen.html>Synoniemen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li>snoodaard</li></ul>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Verwante_begrippen"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:verwante.html>Verwante</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:begrippen.html>begrippen</a></i></span></h5>
<ul><li><a href = vnd.unilang:snood.html>snood</a></li></ul>

</body>

***bootreis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bootreis.html>bootreis</a> (54923)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">boat</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:reis.html>reis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***bootstrap.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a> (57976)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">strap</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">bootstraps</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>loop</a> (leather or other material) sewn at the side or top rear of a <a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a> to help in pulling the <a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a> on.</li>
<li>A means of advancing oneself or accomplishing something without aid.
<dl><dd><i>He used his business experience as a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a></b> to win voters.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The process by which the operating system of a computer <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> loaded into its memory</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The process necessary to compile the tools that will be used to compile the <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> of the system or program.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">statistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any method or instance of estimating properties of an estimator (such as its variance) by measuring those properties when sampling from an approximating distribution.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a> aggregating</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a> model</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a> principle</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a> theory</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">pull oneself up by one's bootstraps</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">booting</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cold <a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">bootstraps</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bootstrapping</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">bootstrapped</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To help (oneself) without the aid of others.
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:sam.html>Sam</a> spent years <b>bootstrapping</b> himself through college.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To load the operating system into the memory of a computer. Usually shortened to <i><a href = vnd.unilang:boot.html>boot</a></i>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To compile the tools that will be used to compile the <a href = vnd.unilang:rest.html>rest</a> of the system or program.
<dl><dd><i>Bootstrapping means building the GNU C Library, GNU Compiler Collection and several other key system programs.</i><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.gentoo.org/doc/en/handbook/handbook-x86.xml?part=1amp;chap=6">[1]</a></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">statistics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To employ a <a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a> method.</li>
<li>To expand or advance an activity or a collection based solely on previous actions, work, findings, etc.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b>,  James <a href = vnd.unilang:lambert.html>Lambert</a>,  “A multitude of ‘lishes’: The nomenclature of hybridity”, in  <cite>English World-Wide</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.researchgate.net/publication/318367113_A_multitude_of_lishes_The_nomenclature_of_hybridity">[2]</a></sup>, page 5:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Gradually, more and more <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> discovered, especially as there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> a tendency in the literature to list a number of related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> together, thus allowing <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> to <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bootstrap.html>bootstrap</a></b> new <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> found accompanying those originally searched for.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms_2">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">reboot</span></li></ul>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">burat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">bourras</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">burra</i>.

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:bordeel.html>bordeel</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brothel; <a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a>, hovel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">bordel</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hut.html>hut</a>; brothel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***bordes.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bordes.html>bordes</a> (94957)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">bordessche</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bordes.html>bordes</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bordes.html>bordessen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bordes.html>bordesje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A raised platform, often with a flight of <a href = vnd.unilang:steps.html>steps</a>, that lead into a building</li>
<li>An intermediate platform between <a href = vnd.unilang:flights.html>flights</a> of stairs, which normally involves a change in direction; a landing</li>
<li>A balcony (open or roofed), porch or lean-to.
<ul><li><b>1960</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> Koelewijn, "<a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>Kom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dak.html>dak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a>", <a href = vnd.unilang:peter.html>Peter</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rockets.html>Rockets</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kom.html>Kom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dak.html>dak</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:af.html>af</a></i>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="nl">Jan Janssen z'n <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouw.html>vrouw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> koordanseres, / <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gebrek.html>gebrek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:touw.html>touw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:klom.html>klom</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:bordes.html>bordes</a></b>.</span><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this quote)</small></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">borchtocht</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:borg.html>borg</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tocht.html>tocht</a></i>.

***borscht.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:borscht.html>borscht</a> (65781)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1884 or 1808. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Yiddish" class="extiw" title="w:Yiddish">Yiddish</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="yi">באָרשט</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="yi-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">borsht</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Russian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Russian language">Russian</a></span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">борщ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boršč</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">barszcz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:borscht.html>borscht</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">borschts</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A beetroot soup that can be served hot or cold, usually with sour cream.</li>
<li>Any similar sour soup made of other ingredients such as sorrel, cabbage, hogweed</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">cheap like <a href = vnd.unilang:borscht.html>borscht</a></span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:borscht.html>Borscht</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belt.html>Belt</a></span></li></ul>
</body>

<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:borst.html>borst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">breast</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wering</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:keeping.html>keeping</a> out</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, replacing older <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">borstweer</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:bosbes.html>bosbes</a> (54920)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bos.html>bos</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">forest</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bes.html>bes</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">berry</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>bilberry</li>
<li>bilberry plant, member of the genus <i>Vaccinium</i></li></ol>

<dl><dd><span style="color:0060ff;font-weight: bold;">▸</span> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dagenlang.html>Dagenlang</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:liep.html>liep</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a
